 ) bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ne 'namo tivi' ko media certification and monitering cameti (MCMC) kii manjuuri ke bina hi launch kiya tha
 According to the documents MCMC had rejected the launch request for Namo TV
 bijepi ne MCMC se manjuuri lene kii apil kii thi lekin party kii is maang ko khaarij kar diya gaya tha

 bina anumati hi namo tivi kii lonching karne ko sidhe prakriyaaon kaa ulanghan mana ja rahaa he
 The Media Certification and Monitoring Committee is set up during elections on behalf of the Election Commission at the state and district levels
 aachaar samhita lagu hone ke baad vigyapanon or prachaar aadi kii manjuuri is sanstha kii manjuuri jaruri hoti he
 India Today has documents of this entire controversy
 ye dastavej us dauraan ke hai, jab bhaajapa kii ore se namo tivi kii ijaajat ke liye aavedan kiya gaya tha
 On March 29, an application was received from Neeraj, a member of the Election Commission of the BJP in the concerned department of the Election Commission, to get a certificate of media / advertisement
 is madhyam ko tivi, rath vine, soshal media or cinema (desh bhar main) ke madhyamon se dikhaane kii ijaajat maangi gai thi
 The media certification committee, after examining the contents of this application, had allowed the broadcast on 30 March
 iskaa aashay he ki sirf namo tivi ke logo ko hari jhandi di gai thi
 After this, on March 29, March 30, April 1, April 2, April 3, April 5 and April 8, the concerned department of the Election Commission received 10 applications for certification of media / advertisement of Namo TV, instead of advertising
 There were speeches and interviews
 is aavedan kii mjedaar baat yah thi ki aavedan main piem modi ke bhaashanon ke liye purv ijaajat dene kii maang kii gai thi
 This was not possible because prior permission is given only for programs which are not already in the public domain
 bhaajapa ne apane aavedan main yah nahin bataaya ki isamen bhaashan or documentries dikhaai jaaengi
 Apart from the logo of Namo TV, it did not mention any channel or platform of political advertisement
 aavedan main arun jetali kaa aap kii adaalat main janaa, amit shah kaa india ke diene main janaa, narendra modi kaa abeepi news main intervyuu aadi ke prasaaran kii baat kahi gai thi
 The Certification Committee could not give their certificate of broadcasting, as they were already in the public domain
 is aavedan or isaki saamagree kii jaanch ke baad cameti ko laga tha ki yah kisi tarah kaa raajnneetik vigyaapan nahin he, isliye tay hua ki yah cameti is par nirnay nahin le sakati he
 This clearly means that the certificate was not given for the speech or interview
 is bare main aavedak ko bataa bhi diya gaya tha
 There was correspondence on April 3, April 6 and April 8
 iske baad bhaajapa kii ore se is bare main koi jawaab nahin diya gaya tha
 Namo TV is still airing and currently no order has been issued by the Election Commission to stop the broadcast of this TV
